BOOKS FROM NOTRE DAME 
The Bible and the Liturgy Jean Danielou, S. J. 
The ~acramental rites of the Church-Baptism, Con­firmation, Holy Eucharist and great feasts of the liturgi­cal year-were designed to be an unfailing source of grace and meaning in the Christian life. Now due to lack of instruction, the rites are too often seen 'as curi­osities with no message for today's Christians. To remedy this situation Father Danielou examines the sign language of the Sacraments via modem scholar­ship in easily understandable language. This study will prove invaluable to those interested in learning and teaching the meaning of Christianity. October. $5.25 
Christian Democracy in Western Europe, 1814-1952 
M. P. Fogarty 
A comprehensive study of the Christian Democratic movements in England, France, Italy, Germany, Bel­gium and the Netherlands. The author has not limited himself to a political history, but has compiled a far­ranging account of the richness of Christian Democratic social thought. December. $6.75 
The Fate of East Central Europe; Hopes and Failures of American Foreign Policy 
Edited by Stephen D. Kertesz 
How the nations of East Central Europe came under Communist domination and what part American policy played in this vital area is the subject of this book. President Emeritus Charles Seymour of Yale says, "This book faces courageously and objectively lhe critical issue of United States policy toward East Central Europe. It provides the historical background essential to an understanding of the issue ... The distinction of the authors of the various chapters assures the validity of their approach to this vital problem." 
October. $6.25 

The Ancrene Riwle 
Edited and translated by M. B. Salu 
The complete text in modern English of this classic of mediaeval spirituality, with critical notes and references. The book contains a preface by Professor J. R. R. Tolkien and an introduction and appendix by Dom Gerard Sitwell. October. $2.75 


RECENTLY PUBLISHED 
The Mystery of the Woman 
Edited by Edward D. O'Connor, C.S.C. 
A simple and profound explanation of the three Marian dogmas which have made the greatest impact on the life of the Church, written by three outstanding Ameri­can Theologians, Walter Burghardt, S.J., Ferrer Smith, O.P., and Monsignor George Shea. $2.75 
Church Building and Furnishing 
J. B. O'Connell 
An indispensable tool for pastor and architect-the only one-volume book that brings together all the official regulations governing the building, furnishing and decorating of Catholic Churches. This compact refer­ance work contains, in an orderly and readily accessible form, the canons, rubrics and prescriptions concerningchurch architecture. The book's many beautiful illus­trations will prove of great va1ue by demonstrating how wide is the range of technical s1:,lutions open to those who wish to build in accordance with the mind of the Church. 44 Wustrations. $5.50 

Liturgical Piety Pere Louis Bouyer 
Our Land and Our Lady 

Daniel Sargent 
Traces the hand of Our Lady through the early history of America. Mr. Sargent interprets early beginnings and the later history of Catholicism in this country in terms of Our Blessed Mother. The struggle for Catholic edu­cation is well brought out. This story of missionary beginnings, strivings, failures and ultimate success is told with _profound spirituality. $3.50 
Men in the Field 

Leo J. Ward, C.S.C. 
18 powerful short stories of Midwestern farm life of a generation ago. A cross section of life is laid bare-the people in all their pitiful and wonderful human variety are viewed with compassion and respect, portrayed with tenderness and strength. Father Ward's realistic stories hold more than the exact detail of corn farm life, they hold its spirit. $3.50 
Published only last year, it has already been hailed a work of permanent importance and acclaimed an indispensable book for the clergy and the educated laity. The study re­examines the nature and history of the Christian liturgy from its Jewish roots to its present status. Liturgical experts say: Jungman, S.J. "... this courageous book ... this majestic conception." Howell "..• a major event in the Catholic world of letters.." Quasten "..• a work of lasting value." $4.75
